msg:We had the highest expectations for this hotel during the entire trip, because considering that Xichang is most famous for Qionghai Lake, we booked a sea view room without hesitation. When we arrived at the hotel, we found that this hotel is divided into many hotel areas, similar to the local high-end guesthouse, where many important meetings are held and there are abundant customers. To be honest, this hotel has a first-class environment and beautiful scenery. Our Wangyue Building is downstairs from Qionghai Lake. But when we entered the sea view room we booked, we felt very disappointed: the room was small and the facilities were very traditional. The key point was that although the bathroom was clean, it was estimated that the drainage system was old and had a bad smell. The breakfast was very simple and rough, and it was inconvenient to eat. It took 3-5 minutes to walk to the centralized dining point. The key point was that the food was as rough as the tourist meals of 2-3 star hotels. Thanks to the fact that Qionghai Lake is really beautiful, the hotel has unique conditions, which diluted our disappoin**ent.

msg:The hotel is really great, very big, you can go anywhere, just play in the hotel and nearby, next time you come to Xichang, I will definitely choose Qionghai Hotel. [Play] Go out the back door to Qionghai, really zero distance; turn right and walk along Qionghai for five minutes to the style town, various restaurants; turn left and walk for ten minutes to Diaoyutai. It takes 10 minutes to walk from the South Gate to Lushan. There is a car rental shop on the left side of the South Gate with a very reasonable price. Rent a car and go south, ride along the shore of Qionghai. There are very few people after the banyan garden. Cycling, taking pictures, playing in the sand, fishing, and skipping stones are very good. [Eat] There are many restaurants near the hotel, but they are all thunder. I sincerely advise everyone to eat in the hotel. The buffet, Western food, snacks, barbecue, and Chinese food taste very good, and the price is not expensive (you can join the WeChat group). [Live] Needless to say, the hotel environment is super good. You can swim, play in the water, soak in hot springs (hot pools), drink afternoon tea and watch the sea view, eat barbecue and blow the sea breeze at night, and play directly in the hotel; the newly renovated room is very good, the only drawback is that the pillow is too soft, I hope it can be improved. [Travel] It is very convenient to take a taxi directly at the South Gate; you can rent a bicycle and ride around the sea, or ride directly to the old town to buy some fruit and have a meal.
